# Тоталитаризм – моральный банкрот
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.0
	title = NW_JAP_looser.0.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.0" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.0.a
		add_stability = 0.15
	}
}

		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party7 name = JAP_fascism_party7 }
	}
}

# Массовые митинги на улицах
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.8
	title = NW_JAP_looser.8.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
			has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
		}
		has_idea = JAP_growth_of_party_combat_organizations_idea
		has_stability < 0.15
		fascism > 0.25
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.8" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.8.a
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP_looser.9 days = 1 } }
	}
}

# Ошибочное предсказание
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.11
	title = NW_JAP_looser.11.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.11" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.11.a
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = -0.25
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				OR = {
					capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
					original_tag = USA
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_embrace_pacifism_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_looser.12
	title = NW_JAP_looser.12.t
	desc = NW_JAP_looser.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_looser.12" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP_looser.13 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_looser.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ENG }

					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }

					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
			286 = {
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
			741 = {
				if = {
					limit = { controller = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
			1179 = {
				if = {

					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}

			1180 = {

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.7
	title = NW_JAP.7.t
	desc = NW_JAP.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { NOT = { has_government = monarchy } }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.7" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.7.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.02 }
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party1_long name = JAP_fascism_party1 }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Seigo_Nakano
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = totalism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_supporter_of_parliamentary_politics JAP_charismatic_agitator }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.317 days = 60 } }
	}
}

# Новый Токио
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.8
	title = NW_JAP.8.t
	desc = NW_JAP.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.8" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.8.a
		add_ideas = JAP_construction_of_the_new_tokyo_idea
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_new_capital_tt
		hidden_effect = { set_province_name = { id = 7157 name = JAP_new_capital } }
		set_capital = { state = 532 }
		532 = {
			add_victory_points = {
				province = 7157
				value = 30
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = supply_node
				province = 7157
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = fuel_silo
						size > 4
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.8.b
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.27

	desc = NW_JAP.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.27.a
		SHA = {
			transfer_state = 597
			transfer_state = 743
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = SHA_jan_tsunyan
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = SHA_jan_tsunyan
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}

					promote_leader = yes

					}

# Создание Империи Хань
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.29
	title = NW_JAP.29.t
	desc = NW_JAP.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.29" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.29.a
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			ROOT = {
				every_controlled_state = {
					limit = { OR = { is_core_of = HCP is_core_of = EHB is_core_of = SHX } }
					transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_the_Great_Han_State
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 1	}
				set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = CSR_neutrality_party3 name = CSR_neutrality_party3 }
			hidden_effect = { CSR = { CSR_van_in = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV } } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = CSR_van_in
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = despotism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
#			load_focus_tree = 
#			complete_national_focus = 
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.28.b
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			ROOT = {

					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_the_Great_Han_State
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
				add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 1	}
				set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = CSR_neutrality_party3 name = CSR_neutrality_party3 }
			hidden_effect = { CSR = { CSR_van_in = { set_nationality = PREV.PREV } } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = CSR_van_in
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = despotism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
#			load_focus_tree = 
#			complete_national_focus = 
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}

	id = NW_JAP.35

		text = NW_JAP.35.t.a
		trigger = { original_tag = JAP }
	}
	title = {
		text = NW_JAP.35.t.b
		trigger = { original_tag = SOV }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.35.d.a
		trigger = { original_tag = JAP }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.35.d.b
		trigger = { original_tag = SOV }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		JAP = {
			check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 10 }
			all_enemy_country = { is_major = no }
			controls_state = 527
		}
		SOV = { 
			controls_state = 984
			all_enemy_country = { is_major = no }
			has_civil_war = no
		}
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.35" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.35.a
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = JAP }
			activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen
			SOV = { activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen }
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen
				JAP = { activate_mission = JAP_preparing_for_Chankufen }
			}
		}
	}
}

# JAP Согласие китайского правительства на перемирие
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.47
	title = NW_JAP.47.t
	desc = NW_JAP.47.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.47" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.47.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = -1
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { is_literally_china = yes }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = { annex_country = { target = HCP transfer_troops = yes } }
		1031 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1145 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		608 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1132 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MEN }
			MEN = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CSR }
			CSR = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.0 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.47.b
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 1145
			controls_state = 1031
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.51 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { original_tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		annex_country = { target = HCP transfer_troops = yes }
		1031 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1145 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		608 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1132 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MEN }
			MEN = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CSR }
			CSR = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.53.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.50 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.77
	title = NW_JAP.77.t
	desc = NW_JAP.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.77" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.77.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
			country_event = { id = NW_JAP.76 hours = 6 }
			else = {
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_restavration_Seva_Reiva } } complete_national_focus = JAP_restavration_Seva_Reiva }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life } } complete_national_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_imperial_support_for_reforms } } complete_national_focus = JAP_imperial_support_for_reforms }
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_invite_Ikki_Kita } } complete_national_focus = JAP_invite_Ikki_Kita }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Начало Реставрации Сёва/Рейва
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.78
	title = {
		text = NW_JAP.78.t.a
		trigger = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
	}
	title = {
		text = NW_JAP.78.t.b
		trigger = { has_idea = JAP_Reiva }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.78.d.a
		trigger = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
	}
	desc = {
		text = NW_JAP.78.d.b
		trigger = { has_idea = JAP_Reiva }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.78" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.78.a
		add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_the_threat_of_radicalization_of_young_officers days = 30 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
			add_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva
			else = { add_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva }
		}
	}
}

# Император отправляет премьер-министра в отставку
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.79
	title = NW_JAP.79.t
	desc = NW_JAP.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_idea = JAP_Reiva }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.79" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.79.a
		hidden_effect = {
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_moderate_political_reform
			uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = JAP_moderate_political_reform }
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life } } complete_national_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life }
		complete_national_focus = JAP_Yasuhito_direct_rule
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.79.b
		hidden_effect = {
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_moderate_political_reform
			uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = JAP_moderate_political_reform }
		}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life } } complete_national_focus = JAP_increase_the_participation_of_the_Emperor_in_political_life }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_imperial_support_for_reforms } } complete_national_focus = JAP_imperial_support_for_reforms }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_invite_Ikki_Kita } } complete_national_focus = JAP_invite_Ikki_Kita }
	}
}

# Арест молодых офицеров
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.80
	title = NW_JAP.80.t
	desc = NW_JAP.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki ruling_only = yes } }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.80" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.80.a
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -15 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_the_threat_of_a_counter_coup }
			add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = JAP_the_threat_of_a_counter_coup days = -30 }
		}
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.81
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.81"
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_get_rid_of_radical_elements } }
			unlock_national_focus = JAP_collusion_with_some_of_the_old_elites
			uncomplete_national_focus = { focus = JAP_collusion_with_some_of_the_old_elites }
			country_event = NW_JAP.77
		}
	}
}

# Выборы после периода чрезвычайного положения
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.82
	title = NW_JAP.82.t
	desc = NW_JAP.82.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.82" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.82.a
		set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Machida_Chuji
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = social_liberalism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_a_staunch_commoner JAP_progressive }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_tt
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Kadsucige_Ugaki
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Mitsumasa_Yonai
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Gotaro_Ogava
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Nakadzima_Yadanji
		show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Eikiti_Katsuta
	}
}

# Окава полностью свободен
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.83
	title = NW_JAP.83.t
	desc = NW_JAP.83.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.83" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.83.a
		set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party2_long name = JAP_fascism_party2 }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Shumei_Okawa
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = national_socialism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_leader_of_the_Pan_Asian_movement JAP_political_conspirator_and_ideologue }
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } }
			ROOT = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = PREV
					value = 50
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = area_priority
					id = asia
					value = 75
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.88 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			}
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = CSR }
				CSR = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# JAP Встреча в Сан-Франциско
news_event = {
	id = NW_JAP_news.7
	title = NW_JAP_news.7.t
	desc = NW_JAP_news.7.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_dutch_soldiers_indonesia
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP_news.7" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_news.7.a
		trigger = { OR = { original_tag = USA original_tag = JAP } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_news.7.b
		trigger = { OR = { tag = event_target:NW_france_scope original_tag = ENG } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_news.7.c
		trigger = { NOT = { original_tag = USA original_tag = JAP tag = event_target:NW_france_scope original_tag = ENG has_government = communism } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP_news.7.d
		trigger = { has_government = communism }
	}
}

# JAP Согласие США на переговоры
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.102
	title = NW_JAP.102.t
	desc = NW_JAP.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.102" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.102.a
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.105 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = enemies
					has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					has_country_flag = china_declare_government_flag
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.106 days = 4 random_days = 3 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { is_literally_china = yes is_faction_leader = yes has_war_with = ROOT }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.106 days = 4 random_days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.102.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.103 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.8 days = 1 } }
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_embargoing = FROM }
				break_embargo = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.106.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		USA = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.107 days = 1 } }
	}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.121
	title = NW_JAP.121.t
	desc = NW_JAP.121.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.121" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.121.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hideki_Todze ruling_only = yes } } }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Hideki_Todze
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_representative_of_Toseikha }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Todze_office } }
			complete_national_focus = JAP_Todze_office
		}
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_operation_Z_category
		activate_mission = JAP_tora_tora_tora
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.121.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.123 days = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 20 } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.137 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		text = NW_JAP.126.d.b
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe ruling_only = yes } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.126" }

			limit = { NOT = { has_government = neutrality } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Hideki_Todze ruling_only = yes } } }
			effect_tooltip = {

					character = JAP_Hideki_Todze

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Todze_office } }
			complete_national_focus = JAP_Todze_office
		}
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_operation_Z_category
		activate_mission = JAP_tora_tora_tora
	}
	option = {

		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Fumimaro_Konoe ruling_only = yes } }

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.128
	title = NW_JAP.128.t
	desc = NW_JAP.128.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.128" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.128.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var < 10 } }
		FIC = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_japanese_occupation }
				remove_ideas = JAP_japanese_occupation
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = ROOT }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			event_target:NW_france_scope = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.129 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.128.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.135 days = 1 } }
	}
}

# CHI Американцы предлагают посредничество
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.131
	title = NW_JAP.131.t
	desc = NW_JAP.131.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.131" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.131.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.10 days = 1 } }
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_embargoing = FROM }
				break_embargo = FROM
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = JAP_the_Great_Peacemaker
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.132 days = 20 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.131.b
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.11 days = 1 } }
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_embargoing = FROM }
				break_embargo = FROM
			}
		}
		FIC = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_japanese_occupation }
				remove_ideas = JAP_japanese_occupation
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_military_access_to = FROM }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = FROM }
				FROM = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			event_target:NW_france_scope = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_Asian_Switzerland_idea
		}
	}
}

				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.133 days = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var > 20 } check_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var < 30 } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.134 days = 1 }
			}
		}	
	}
}

# Покушение на принца
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.133
	title = NW_JAP.133.t
	desc = NW_JAP.133.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.133" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.133.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.12 days = 1 } }
		kill_country_leader = yes
		retire_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = -15 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka ruling_only = yes } } }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Yosuke_Matsuoka
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_former_President_of_Mantetsu JAP_master_of_a_Hundred_Thousand_Words }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office } }
				complete_national_focus = JAP_Matsuoka_Office
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito ruling_only = yes } } }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_bad_reputation_in_the_imperial_house JAP_liberal_imperialist JAP_a_mad_political_schemer }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_Naruhiko_office } }
				complete_national_focus = JAP_Naruhiko_office
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.160
	title = NW_JAP.160.t
	desc = NW_JAP.160.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.160" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.160.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.15 days = 35 } }
		FROM = {
			#MON и JAP
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		MAN = {
			#MON и MAN
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = FROM
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = FROM
			}
			#SOV и MAN
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = SOV
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_op
				target = SOV
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			#SOV и клики
			limit = { is_literally_china = yes NOT = { original_tag = MON original_tag = MAN is_subject_of = ROOT is_subject_of = SOV } }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = SOV
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = SOV
			}
			#JAP и клики
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_recognition_of_Manchukuo_and_MNR_2_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

		name = NW_JAP.187.a

		set_country_flag = JAP_reform_of_common_affairs_UNLOCK_flag
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = JAP_reform_of_common_affairs }
	}

		trigger = { has_country_flag = JAP_Hirota_Koki_has_resigned_flag }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.187.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_Hirota_Koki_has_resigned_flag }
			has_country_flag = JAP_concessions_to_the_military_flag

# Скелеты в шкафу
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.197
	title = NW_JAP.197.t
	desc = NW_JAP.197.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.197" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.197.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = monarchy popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.02 }
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_last_war }
			set_country_flag = JAP_Satomi_Katoshi_flag
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = JAP_Satomi_Katoshi
			else = {

	id = NW_JAP.231
	title = NW_JAP.231.t
	desc = NW_JAP.231.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.231" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.231.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { original_tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		annex_country = { target = HCP transfer_troops = yes }
		1031 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1145 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		608 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1132 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MEN }
			MEN = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CSR }
			CSR = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.48 hours = 6 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.30 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.231.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.232 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.269
	title = NW_JAP.269.t
	desc = NW_JAP.269.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.269" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.269.a
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.40 days = 1 } }
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { original_tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = { NOT = { state = 525 state = 527 state = 528 state = 529 state = 530 state = 531 state = 532 state = 533 state = 534 state = 535 state = 536 state = 471 state = 282 } }
				transfer_state_to = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.269.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.271 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.269.c
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.270 days = 1 } }
	}
}

		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 5 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = JAP_purge_of_Kodoha_members_in_the_Army_flag } }
				set_character_flag = JAP_mass_killings_in_Nanjing_flag
				effect_tooltip = { retire = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.273.b
		add_to_variable = { JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var = 15 tooltip = JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_var_tt }
		JAP_the_level_of_insubordination_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.274 days = 30 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.295
	title = NW_JAP.295.t
	desc = NW_JAP.295.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.295" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.295.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		load_focus_tree = nw_japan_looser_focus
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.47 days = 1 }
			FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.297 days = 2 } }
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_literally_china = yes is_in_faction_with = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } }
			white_peace = { tag = ROOT }
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
			ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			FROM = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { OR = { is_literally_china = yes tag = KOR } }
			every_core_state = {
				limit = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
				transfer_state_to = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.295.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -10
				enemies_strength_ratio > 2
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.296 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.297
	title = NW_JAP.297.t
	desc = NW_JAP.297.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = KOR } }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.297" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.297.a
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = KOR }
			transfer_state_to = KOR
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory" has_dlc = "Man the Guns" } }
			set_autonomy = { target = KOR autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
			else = { puppet = KOR }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.297.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = KOR }
			transfer_state_to = KOR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.297.c
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -35
	}
}

			}
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -6
				enemies_strength_ratio > 1
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -4
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = NW_JAP_news.53 days = 1 } }
		FROM = {
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				white_peace = { tag = PREV }
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = { capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia } NOT = { original_tag = MAN } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
		MAN = {
			if = {
				limit = { exists = yes }
				ROOT = { NW_remove_unrecognized_effect = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.315.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.316 days = 1 } }
	}

# Подготовительный комитет
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.323
	title = NW_JAP.323.t
	desc = NW_JAP.323.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.323" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.323.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_people_Savings_Promotion_Company }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.324 days = 10 }	#Окружение Коноэ поддерживает Накано
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.325 days = 10 }	#Новая Обновленческая партия сформирована
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_take_a_tough_anti_war_stance }
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.327 days = 10 }	#Нерешённый вопрос
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.323.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes }
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_b_event_flag
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.327 days = 10 }	#Нерешённый вопрос
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.323.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes }
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_319_c_event_flag
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag } }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.325 days = 10 }	#Новая Обновленческая партия сформирована
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.328 days = 10 }	#Коллективное руководство новой партией
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag }
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.326 days = 10 }	#Напряжённость в переговорах
				}

# Новая обновленческая партия сформирована
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.325
	title = NW_JAP.325.t
	desc = NW_JAP.325.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.325" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.325.a
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_325_event_flag
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_fascism_party6 name = JAP_fascism_party6 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_325_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp = JAP_tohokai_popularity }
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity_temp = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp tooltip = NW_JAP_325_toh_tt }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity_temp tooltip = NW_JAP_325_st_tt }
			clear_variable = JAP_tohokai_popularity
			clear_variable = JAP_shakai_taishuto_popularity
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_320_event_flag }
				custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_325_event_tt_2
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp = JAP_small_parties_popularity }
				divide_temp_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp = 2 }
				round_temp_variable = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp
				add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp tooltip = NW_JAP_325_sp_tt }
				subtract_from_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp }
			}
			add_to_variable = { JAP_currently_num_parties = -1 }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.329 days = 25 } }		#Противовес Какушин Шинто
		}
	}
}

# Напряжённость в переговорах
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.326
	title = NW_JAP.326.t
	desc = NW_JAP.326.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.326" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.326.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Machida_Chuji ruling_only = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag
						democratic > 0.6
					}
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.330 days = 1 }				#Коноэ возглавит Новую Обновленческую партию
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_9_event_flag }
						has_completed_focus = JAP_parliamentary_elections
						democratic > 0.6
					}
					country_event = { id = NW_JAP.330 days = 1 }				#Коноэ возглавит Новую Обновленческую партию
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.331 days = 1 }						#Совместное заявление
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

# Поездка Накано на фронт
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.334
	title = NW_JAP.334.t
	desc = NW_JAP.334.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_war = yes
		NOT = { has_variable = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity }
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.331" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.334.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.03 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission
				check_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity > 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_334_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp = JAP_tohokai_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp = 2 }
			round_temp_variable = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp
			add_to_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_small_parties_popularity_tt }
			subtract_from_variable = { JAP_tohokai_popularity = JAP_tohokai_popularity_temp }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

	id = NW_JAP.335

	desc = NW_JAP.335.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.335" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.335.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission
				check_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity > 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_335_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp = JAP_small_parties_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp = 2 }
			round_temp_variable = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp
			add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			subtract_from_variable = { JAP_small_parties_popularity = JAP_small_parties_popularity_temp }
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_innovation_alliance_popularity }
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.336 days = 1 }		#Накадзима присоединяется к движению Рютаро
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.337 days = 1 }		#Борьба за депутатов
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_active_mission = JAP_agitation_of_rivals_mission }
			set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = JAP_democratic_party4 name = JAP_democratic_party4 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = NW_JAP_337_event_tt
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_temp = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity }
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_temp = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_temp = 4 }
			round_temp_variable = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_temp
			set_temp_variable = { JAP_sum_of_two_parties = 0 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_sum_of_two_parties = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_temp }
			add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_sum_of_two_parties = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_temp }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = JAP_sum_of_two_parties tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			divide_temp_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_temp = -1 }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_temp tooltip = JAP_kakushin_shinto_popularity_tt }

	title = NW_JAP.359.t
	desc = NW_JAP.359.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_purge_of_Toseiha_members_in_the_Army_country_flag }
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_347_event_flag
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_358_event_flag
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_344_event_flag
		}
	}
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.359" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.359.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_347_event_flag
					has_country_flag = NW_JAP_358_event_flag
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity = 10 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -10 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -10 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_344_event_flag }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_sayukai_reformists_popularity = 7 tooltip = JAP_rikken_sayukai_popularity_tt }
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = JAP_shinshinto_popularity }
				add_to_variable = { JAP_shinshinto_popularity = -7 tooltip = JAP_shinshinto_popularity_tt }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity = -7 tooltip = JAP_rikken_minseito_popularity_tt }
			}
			JAP_Machid_Chunji_office_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Смерть Хисаси Асо
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.371
	title = NW_JAP.371.t
	desc = NW_JAP.371.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.371" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.371.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Aso_Hisashi ruling_only = yes } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Inedziro_Asanuma
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = national_socialism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party21 name = JAP_neutrality_party21 }
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.372 days = 100 } }
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Aso_Hisashi
	}
}

# Смерть Гондо Сэйкё
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.385
	title = NW_JAP.385.t
	desc = NW_JAP.385.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.385" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.385.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_power_balance = { id = JAP_invite_farmers_power_balance } }
			remove_power_balance = { id = JAP_invite_farmers_power_balance }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Gondo_Seike ruling_only = yes } }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki }
					remove_country_leader_role = {
						character = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki
						ideology = monarchy_ideology
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Jinzaburo_Masaki
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = agrarian_nationalism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_hated_by_political_elites JAP_Conflict_with_the_Manchurian_Faction JAP_the_leader_of_Kodoha }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_JAP.386 days = 1 } }
		}
		retire_character = JAP_Gondo_Seike
	}
}

# Угаки уходит
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.384
	title = NW_JAP.384.t
	desc = NW_JAP.384.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = JAP_Kadsucige_Ugaki ruling_only = yes } }
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.384" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.384.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = NW_JAP_300_event_flag
			has_completed_focus = JAP_condemn_the_movement_in_one_party
			power_balance_value = { id = JAP_Hirota_Koki_power_balance value > 0 }
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = -0.1 }
		add_stability = 0.15
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.384.b
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = JAP_preparation_of_Ugaki_heir }
		set_country_flag = JAP_Abe_office_UNLOCK_flag
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = JAP_Abe_office }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_189_c_event_flag }
			promote_character = JAP_Dziro_Minami
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party13 name = JAP_neutrality_party13 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = NW_JAP_189_b_event_flag }
			promote_character = JAP_kuniaki_koiso
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party14 name = JAP_neutrality_party14 }
		}
		else = {
			promote_character = JAP_Nobuyuki_Abe
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party12 name = JAP_neutrality_party12 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.384.c
		promote_character = JAP_Hirota_Koki
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_neutrality_party6 name = JAP_neutrality_party6 }
	}
}

			FROM = { save_event_target_as = alliance_inviter }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.401.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = no
				FROM = { has_war = yes }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = alliance_applicant@ROOT
			FROM = { set_country_flag = alliance_inviter@ROOT }
			news_event = { id = news.289 hours = 12 }
		}
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.401.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 65 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 35 }
			}		
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 5 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 35 }
			}			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value < 65 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_war = yes
				FROM = { has_war = no }
			}

# Отмена монархии
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.434
	title = NW_JAP.434.t
	desc = NW_JAP.434.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.434" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.434.a
		set_country_flag = NW_JAP_434_event_flag
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = democratic } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Ivasaburo_Takano
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = socialism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {  }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Seva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_Seva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva1 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva2 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Seva3 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Seva3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_Reiva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_Reiva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva1 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva2 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva3 }
			remove_ideas = JAP_restavration_of_Reiva3
		}
		add_ideas = JAP_mass_defiance_of_the_occupation_idea
		set_variable = { JAP_power_of_resistance_var = 6 }
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_the_fight_against_the_monarchist_underground_category
		activate_mission = JAP_discontent_of_the_peasants_mission
		activate_mission = JAP_activities_of_religious_radicals_mission
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.majors
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			activate_mission = JAP_activities_of_communist_underground_mission
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
					has_government = communism
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.452 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = anarchism }
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.majors
					has_government = anarchism
				}
			}
			activate_mission = JAP_activities_of_anarchist_underground_mission
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
					has_government = anarchism
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_JAP.453 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.441" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.441.a
		retire_country_leader = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { can_be_country_leader = JAP_Machida_Chuji } }
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = JAP_Machida_Chuji
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = social_liberalism
					expire = "1965.1.1.1"
					traits = { JAP_a_staunch_commoner JAP_progressive }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { promote_character = JAP_Machida_Chuji }
	}
}

# Формирование Реформированного правительства Китайской Республики I
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.442
	title = NW_JAP.442.t
	desc = NW_JAP.442.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.442" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.442.a
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			add_political_power = 100
			transfer_state = 613
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger" }
					set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_subject }
					else = { puppet = PREV }
				}
				set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = JAP_Tan_Shaoi }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_reformed_government_of_the_republic_of_china
			if = { 
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Tan_Shaoi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nationalism_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }

					character = JAP_Tan_Shaoi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy

						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}

					character = JAP_Tan_Shaoi

			set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_reformed_government_of_the_republic_of_china

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.444
	title = NW_JAP.444.t
	desc = NW_JAP.444.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.444" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.444.a
		country_event = { id = NW_JAP.445 hours = 12 }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.445
	title = NW_JAP.445.t
	desc = NW_JAP.445.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = NW_JAP.445.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.03 }
		add_country_leader_trait = JAP_supporter_of_the_ideas_of_coudenhove_kalergi
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = asia }
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					has_opinion_modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_create_a_brotherhood_op
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

# Восстание крестьян
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.448
	title = NW_JAP.448.t
	desc = NW_JAP.448.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.448"
		hidden_effect = {
			MPJ = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_country_with_original_tag = {
							original_tag_to_check = ROOT 
							has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
						}
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							has_character = JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi
						}
						JAP_Masanobu_Cudzi = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = absolute_monarchy
									expire = "1965.1.1.1"
									traits = {  }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					promote_character = JAP_Takusiro_Hattori
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Showa Defenders" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Showa Defenders"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = num_controlled_states }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_power_of_resistance_var > 7 } }
						divide_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 1.66 }
						PREV = { set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 20 } }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_power_of_resistance_var > 3 } }
						divide_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 2 }
						PREV = { set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 13 } }
					}
					else = {
						divide_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 3 }
						PREV = { set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 8 } }
					}
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp > 0 } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = -1 }
						random_controlled_state = {
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
					PREV = {
						while_loop_effect = {
							limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
							add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
							random_controlled_state = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"Righteous Army\" division_template = \"Showa Defenders\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
									owner = PREV
									count = 1
								}
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = PREV
						size = 0.5
						stockpile_ratio = 0.4
						army_ratio = 0.4
						air_ratio = 0.4
						navy_ratio = 0.4
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							is_country_leader = no
							is_advisor = no
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.448.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.448.b
		MPJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Восстание секты Нитирэн
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.449
	title = NW_JAP.449.t
	desc = NW_JAP.449.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.449"
		hidden_effect = {
			FPJ = {
				transfer_state = 535
				set_province_controller = 4100
				set_province_controller = 7016
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						has_character = JAP_Nisse_Inoye
					}
					set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = JAP_Nisse_Inoye }
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						has_character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara
					}
					set_nationality = { target_country = PREV character = JAP_Kanji_Ishiwara }									
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = JAP_Nisse_Inoye
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = nichirenism
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Nithirenists" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Nithirenists"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 4 }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
					random_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Nithirenists\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
							owner = PREV
							count = 1
						}
					}
				}				
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.449.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.449.b
		FPJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

						}
					}
					random_other_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							has_character = JAP_Kenzo_Yamamoto
						}
						JAP_Kenzo_Yamamoto = {
							set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							add_country_leader_role = {
								promote_leader = yes
								country_leader = {
									ideology = marxism
									expire = "1965.1.1.1"
									traits = {  }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					promote_character = JAP_Sandzo_Nosaka
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Red Brigades" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Red Brigades"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var > 4 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 4 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 4 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var > 2 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 3 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 3 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var > 0 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 2 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 2 }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 1 }
					}
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp > 0 } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = -1 }
						random_controlled_state = {
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 3 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = ROOT.JAP_num_helpls_for_commi_var }
				while_loop_effect = {
					limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp > 0 } }
					add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = -1 }
					random_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Red Brigades\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
							owner = PREV
							count = 1
						}
					}
				}			
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.450.a		
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.450.b
		CPJ = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Восстание коммунистов
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.451
	title = NW_JAP.451.t
	desc = NW_JAP.451.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.451"
		hidden_effect = {
			APJ = {
				promote_character = JAP_Sandzo_Nosaka
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Red Brigades" } }
					division_template = {
						name = "Red Brigades"
						is_locked = yes
						division_names_group = JAP_INF_01
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var > 4 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 4 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 4 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var > 2 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 3 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 3 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { JAP_num_helpls_for_anarchists_var > 0 }
							check_variable = { num_controlled_states > 2 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 2 }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = 1 }
					}
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = { check_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp > 0 } }
						add_to_temp_variable = { JAP_num_controlled_states_temp = -1 }
						random_controlled_state = {
							transfer_state_to = PREV.PREV
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { JAP_num_divisions_for_spam_temp = 3 }

							count = 1

				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = { add_core_of = PREV.PREV }
					declare_war_on = { target = PREV type = civil_war }
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = ROOT NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = PREV
					PREV = { add_civil_war_target = PREV }
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				every_enemy_country = {
					every_state = {

							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = PREV }
							controller = { tag = PREV.PREV }
						}
						teleport_armies = {
							limit = { tag = PREV }
							to_state_array = controlled_states
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Коммунистическое подполье в Японии
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.452
	title = NW_JAP.452.t
	desc = NW_JAP.452.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.452" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.452.a
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_assistance_to_the_japanese_communists_category
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = JAP_send_weapons }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = JAP_help_financially }
		}
	}
}

# Анархическое подполье в Японии
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.453
	title = NW_JAP.453.t
	desc = NW_JAP.453.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.453" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.453.a
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = JAP_assistance_to_the_japanese_anarchists_category
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = JAP_send_weapons_1 }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = JAP_help_financially_1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Выбор регента
country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.454
	title = NW_JAP.454.t
	desc = NW_JAP.454.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.454" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.a
		trigger = {
			has_character = JAP_Yasuhito
			JAP_Yasuhito = { NOT = { has_ideology_group = monarchy } }
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Yasuhito
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = pure_socialism
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = { JAP_friendly_with_radical_politicians_and_the_military JAP_reformer }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.b
		trigger = { has_character = JAP_Nobuhito }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Nobuhito
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = monarchy_ideology
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {  }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.c
		trigger = { has_character = JAP_Takahito }
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = JAP_Takahito
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = monarchy_ideology
				expire = "1965.1.1.1"
				traits = {  }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.454.d
		trigger = { has_character = JAP_Prince_Naruhito }
		JAP_Prince_Naruhito = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ideology_group = monarchy } }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = monarchy_ideology
						expire = "1965.1.1.1"
						traits = { JAP_bad_reputation_in_the_imperial_house JAP_liberal_imperialist JAP_a_mad_political_schemer }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				promote_character = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_JAP.455
	title = NW_JAP.455.t
	desc = NW_JAP.455.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_cabinet_de_geer
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_JAP.455" }
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.455.a
		add_stability = -0.35
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.455.b
		add_stability = -0.15
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_JAP.455.c
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = -40
	}
}
